WITH target_btcusdt AS (
                                    SELECT coin_pair AS btcusdt_coin_partition
                                        , to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60) AS btcusdt_trade_datetime
                                        , DATE(to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60)) AS btcusdt_trade_date
                                        , trade_minute AS btcusdt_trade_minute
                                        , bids_top_price AS btcusdt_bids_top_price
                                        , (asks_top_price - bids_top_price) AS btcusdt_bid_ask_spread
                                        , (asks_top_price + bids_top_price) / 2 AS btcusdt_bid_ask_average_price
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_top_price AS btcusdt_asks_top_price
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS btcusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_std AS btcusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                    FROM binance.orderbook 
                                    WHERE coin_pair = 'btcusdt'
                                    
                                    ),alt_ethusdt AS (
                                    SELECT coin_pair AS ethusdt_coin_partition
                                        , to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60) AS ethusdt_trade_datetime
                                        , DATE(to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60)) AS ethusdt_trade_date
                                        , trade_minute AS ethusdt_trade_minute
                                        , bids_top_price AS ethusdt_bids_top_price
                                        , (asks_top_price - bids_top_price) AS ethusdt_bid_ask_spread
                                        , (asks_top_price + bids_top_price) / 2 AS ethusdt_bid_ask_average_price
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_top_price AS ethusdt_asks_top_price
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS ethusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_std AS ethusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                    FROM binance.orderbook 
                                    WHERE coin_pair = 'ethusdt'
                                    
                                    ),through_ethbtc AS (
                                    SELECT coin_pair AS ethbtc_coin_partition
                                        , to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60) AS ethbtc_trade_datetime
                                        , DATE(to_timestamp(trade_minute * 60)) AS ethbtc_trade_date
                                        , trade_minute AS ethbtc_trade_minute
                                        , bids_top_price AS ethbtc_bids_top_price
                                        , (asks_top_price - bids_top_price) AS ethbtc_bid_ask_spread
                                        , (asks_top_price + bids_top_price) / 2 AS ethbtc_bid_ask_average_price
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , bids_cum_5000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_10000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_20000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_50000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_100000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , bids_cum_200000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_top_price AS ethbtc_asks_top_price
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_10000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_20000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg AS ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg
                                        , asks_cum_5000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_10000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_10000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_20000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_20000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_50000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_100000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_std
                                        , asks_cum_200000_weighted_std AS ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std
                                    FROM binance.orderbook 
                                    WHERE coin_pair = 'ethbtc'
                                    
                                    )
                                , target_btcusdt_std_dev AS (
                                    SELECT btcusdt_trade_minute AS sd_btcusdt_trade_minute ,
                                        
                                          AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 1 preceding and current row) AS prev_1_btcusdt_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg,
                                          AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 3 preceding and current row) AS prev_3_btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 3 preceding and current row) AS prev_3_btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 3 preceding and current row) AS prev_3_btcusdt_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 3 preceding and current row) AS prev_3_btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 3 preceding and current row) AS prev_3_btcusdt_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg

                                          AVG(btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY btcusdt_coin_partition ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC rows between 5 preceding and current row) AS prev_5_btcusdt_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg

                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 240 preceding and current row) AS prev_240_ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 240 preceding and current row) AS prev_240_ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg,
                                          AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 480 preceding and current row) AS prev_480_ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg,
                                          AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 960 preceding and current row) AS prev_960_ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg,
                                          AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_bids_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_bids_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_asks_cum_50000_weighted_std_avg 
                                        , AVG(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std) OVER (PARTITION BY ethbtc_coin_partition ORDER BY ethbtc_trade_minute ASC rows between 2000 preceding and current row) AS prev_2000_ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_std_avg
                                    FROM through_ethbtc 
                                    )

                                        ,((ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg - LEAD(ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg, 2000) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC)) 
                                            / LEAD(ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg, 2000) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC)) * 100 AS prev_2000_ethbtc_asks_cum_100000_weighted_avg_perc_chg
                                        ,((ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg - LEAD(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg, 2000) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC)) 
                                            / LEAD(ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg, 2000) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC)) * 100 AS prev_2000_ethbtc_asks_cum_200000_weighted_avg_perc_chg
                                        , ((LEAD(ethbtc_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg, 2000) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC) - ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg) 
                                            / ethbtc_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg) * 100 AS prev_ethbtc_2000_askbid_cum_5000_weighted_avg_perc_chg 
                                ,((LAG(btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg, 6) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC) - btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg) / btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg * 100) AS futr_6_askbid_cum_5000_weighted_avg_perc_chg,((LAG(btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg, 8) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC) - btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg) / btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg * 100) AS futr_8_askbid_cum_5000_weighted_avg_perc_chg,((LAG(btcusdt_bids_cum_5000_weighted_avg, 10) OVER (ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute DESC) - btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg) / btcusdt_asks_cum_5000_weighted_avg * 100) AS futr_10_askbid_cum_5000_weighted_avg_perc_chg
                            FROM target_btcusdt LEFT JOIN target_btcusdt_std_dev ON target_btcusdt.btcusdt_trade_minute = target_btcusdt_std_dev.sd_btcusdt_trade_minute LEFT JOIN alt_ethusdt ON target_btcusdt.btcusdt_trade_minute = alt_ethusdt.ethusdt_trade_minute LEFT JOIN alt_ethusdt_std_dev ON target_btcusdt.btcusdt_trade_minute = alt_ethusdt_std_dev.sd_ethusdt_trade_minute LEFT JOIN through_ethbtc ON target_btcusdt.btcusdt_trade_minute = through_ethbtc.ethbtc_trade_minute LEFT JOIN through_ethbtc_std_dev ON target_btcusdt.btcusdt_trade_minute = through_ethbtc_std_dev.sd_ethbtc_trade_minute
                            ORDER BY btcusdt_trade_minute ASC
